data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"#include \u0026quot;AlashMotorControlLite.h\u0026quot;\n\nAlashMotorControlLite motor(DIR_PWM, 4, 3);\n\nvoid smoothSpeed(int target, int delayMs) {\n  int data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"#include \u0026quot;AlashMotorControlLite.h\u0026quot;\n\nAlashMotorControlLite motorFL(PWM_PWM, 32, 33);  // Front Left\nAlashMotorControlLite motorFR(PWM_PWM, 25, 26);  // Front Right\nAlashMotorControlLite motorRL(PWM_PWM, 19, 18);  // Rear Left\nAlashMotorControlLite motorRR(PWM_PWM, 17, 16);  // Rear Right\n\nvoid mecanumDrive(int vx, int vy, int rotation) {\n  int speedFL = vx + vy + rotation;\n  int speedFR = vx - vy - rotation;\n  int speedRL = vx - vy + rotation;\n  int speedRR = vx + vy - rotation;\n\n  motorFL.setSpeed(constrain(speedFL, -100, 100));\n  motorFR.setSpeed(constrain(speedFR, -100, 100));\n  motorRL.setSpeed(constrain(speedRL, -100, 100));\n  motorRR.setSpeed(constrain(speedRR, -100, 100));\n}\n\nvoid setup() {}\n\nvoid loop() {\n  mecanumDrive(50, 0, 0);     // Вперед\n  delay(2000);\n\n  mecanumDrive(0, 50, 0);     // Страфинг влево\n  delay(2000);\n\n  mecanumDrive(0, 0, 30);     // Поворот на месте\n data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"void safeReverse(int newSpeed) {\n  // Текущая скорость\n  int current = motor.getSpeed();\n\n  // Если разные знаки - нужен реверс\n  if ((current \u0026gt; 0 \u0026amp;\u0026amp; newSpeed \u0026lt; 0) || (current \u0026lt; 0 \u0026amp;\u0026amp; newSpeed \u0026gt; 0)) {\n    // Плавно до нуля\n    while (abs(motor.getSpeed()) \u0026gt; 0) {\n      int Пауза\n    motor.stop();\n    delay(200);\n  }\n\n  // Плавно до новой скорости\n  while (motor.getSpeed() != newSpeed) {\n    int speed = motor.getSpeed();\n    int step = (newSpeed \u0026gt; speed) dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">AlashMotorControlLite</h1><a id="user-content-alashmotorcontrollite" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: AlashMotorControlLite" href="#alashmotorcontrollite"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 <p dir="auto"><a href="https://www.arduino.cc/" rel="nofollow"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/d48f555f07e22c0c677048f838b533b531d2be04b239d681da1476b58ab93452/68747470733a2f2f696d672e736869656c64732e696f2f62616467652f41726475696e6f2d436f6d70617469626c652d626c75652e737667" alt="Arduino" data-canonical-src="https://img.shields.io/badge/Arduino-Compatible-blue.svg" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>
<a href="https://www.espressif.com/" rel="nofollow"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/1382ac5eaf23b0e6e50014c934ba99d2d3f9c918e4fdf301c517c0082b5e2ab3/68747470733a2f2f696d672e736869656c64732e696f2f62616467652f45535033322d537570706f727465642d677265656e2e737667" alt="ESP32" data-canonical-src="https://img.shields.io/badge/ESP32-Supported-green.svg" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>
<a href="https://github.com/Alash-electronics/AlashMotorControlLite"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/8dda647c094d812b2cd144d7ac1a4241e08f3f6c1f100b824c424a63483b6a7d/68747470733a2f2f696d672e736869656c64732e696f2f62616467652f76657273696f6e2d312e302e372d6f72616e67652e737667" alt="Version" data-canonical-src="https://img.shields.io/badge/version-1.0.7-orange.svg" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>
<a href="/Alash-electronics/AlashMotorControlLite/blob/main/LICENSE"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/6581c31c16c1b13ddc2efb92e2ad69a93ddc4a92fd871ff15d401c4c6c9155a4/68747470733a2f2f696d672e736869656c64732e696f2f62616467652f6c6963656e73652d4d49542d626c75652e737667" alt="License" data-canonical-src="https://img.shields.io/badge/license-MIT-blue.svg" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Простая и мощная библиотека для управления DC моторами на Arduino и ESP32</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">Библиотека AlashMotorControlLite предоставляет универсальный интерфейс для управления DC моторами через различные драйверы (L298N, TB6612, ZK-5AD, DRV8833, BTS7960 и другие). Поддерживает Arduino, ESP32 и совместимые платформы.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">🚀 Основные возможности</h2><a id="user-content--основные-возможности" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 🚀 Основные возможности" href="#-основные-возможности"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>✅ <strong>Простой API</strong> - управление скоростью от -100 до 100</li>
<li>✅ <strong>4 режима драйверов</strong> - поддержка всех популярных H-Bridge микросхем</li>
<li>✅ <strong>Кроссплатформенность</strong> - Arduino, ESP32, совместимые платы</li>
<li>✅ <strong>Защита от ошибок</strong> - автоматическое ограничение скорости</li>
<li>✅ <strong>ESP32 3.x готова</strong> - поддержка нового PWM API</li>
<li>✅ <strong>17 примеров</strong> - от базовых до продвинутых (меканум колеса)</li>
<li>✅ <strong>Русская документация</strong> - полная поддержка русского языка</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">📦 Установка</h2><a id="user-content--установка" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 📦 Установка" href="#-установка"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<ol dir="auto">
<li>Откройте Arduino IDE</li>
<li><strong>Скетч</strong> → <strong>Подключить библиотеку</strong> → <strong>Управление библиотеками</strong></li>
<li>Найдите <code>AlashMotorControlLite</code></li>
<li>Нажмите <strong>Установить</strong></li>
<li>Перезапустите Arduino IDE</li>
</ol>

<li>Перезапустите Arduino IDE</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">🎯 Быстрый старт</h2><a id="user-content--быстрый-старт" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 🎯 Быстрый старт" href="#-быстрый-старт"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Простейший пример (Arduino + L298N)</h3><a id="user-content-простейший-пример-arduino--l298n" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Простейший пример (Arduino + L298N)" href="#простейший-пример-arduino--l298n"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++ notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="#include &quot;AlashMotorControlLite.h&quot;

// DIR_DIR_PWM режим: IN1=4, IN2=5, EN=6
AlashMotorControlLite motor(DIR_DIR_PWM, 4, 5, 6);

void setup() {
  // Инициализация не требуется
}

void loop() {
  motor.setSpeed(75);    // Вперед на 75%
  delay(2000);

  motor.setSpeed(-50);   // Назад на 50%
  delay(2000);

  motor.stop();          // Остановка
  delay(1000);
}"><pre>#<span class="pl-k">include</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>AlashMotorControlLite.h<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>

  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Инициализация не требуется</span>
}

  motor.<span class="pl-c1">setSpeed</span>(<span class="pl-c1">75</span>);    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Вперед на 75%</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">delay</span>(<span class="pl-c1">2000</span>);

  motor.<span class="pl-c1">setSpeed</span>(-<span class="pl-c1">50</span>);   <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Назад на 50%</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">delay</span>(<span class="pl-c1">2000</span>);

  motor.<span class="pl-c1">stop</span>();          <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Остановка</span>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">ESP32 + ZK-5AD (PWM_PWM режим)</h3><a id="user-content-esp32--zk-5ad-pwm_pwm-режим" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: ESP32 + ZK-5AD (PWM_PWM режим)" href="#esp32--zk-5ad-pwm_pwm-режим"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++ notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="#include &quot;AlashMotorControlLite.h&quot;

// PWM_PWM режим: IN1=GPIO32, IN2=GPIO33
AlashMotorControlLite motor(PWM_PWM, 32, 33);

void setup() {
  Serial.begin(115200);
}

void loop() {
  motor.setSpeed(100);   // Полная скорость вперед
  delay(2000);

  motor.brake();         // Активное торможение
  delay(500);

  motor.setSpeed(-100);  // Полная скорость назад
  delay(2000);

  motor.stop();          // Свободная остановка
  delay(1000);
}"><pre>#<span class="pl-k">include</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>AlashMotorControlLite.h<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> PWM_PWM режим: IN1=GPIO32, IN2=GPIO33</span>
AlashMotorControlLite <span class="pl-en">motor</span>(PWM_PWM, <span class="pl-c1">32</span>, <span class="pl-c1">33</span>);

<span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">setup</span>() {
  Serial.<span class="pl-c1">begin</span>(<span class="pl-c1">115200</span>);
}

<span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">loop</span>() {
  motor.<span class="pl-c1">setSpeed</span>(<span class="pl-c1">100</span>);   <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Полная скорость вперед</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">delay</span>(<span class="pl-c1">2000</span>);

  motor.<span class="pl-c1">brake</span>();         <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Активное торможение</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">delay</span>(<span class="pl-c1">500</span>);

  motor.<span class="pl-c1">setSpeed</span>(-<span class="pl-c1">100</span>);  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Полная скорость назад</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">delay</span>(<span class="pl-c1">2000</span>);

  motor.<span class="pl-c1">stop</span>();          <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Свободная остановка</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">delay</span>(<span class="pl-c1">1000</span>);
}</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">🎛️ Режимы драйверов (MODE)</h2><a id="user-content-️-режимы-драйверов-mode" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 🎛️ Режимы драйверов (MODE)" href="#️-режимы-драйверов-mode"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Библиотека поддерживает 4 режима для различных типов драйверов:</p>
<markdown-accessiblity-table><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Режим</th>
<th>Пины</th>
<th>PWM</th>
<th>Драйверы</th>
<th>Описание</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><strong>DIR_PWM</strong></td>
<td>2</td>
<td>1</td>
<td>TB6612FNG, DRV8833</td>
<td>1 направление + 1 скорость</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><strong>PWM_PWM</strong></td>
<td>2</td>
<td>2</td>
<td>ZK-5AD, L298N, BTS7960</td>
<td>2 PWM для двунаправленного управления</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><strong>DIR_DIR_PWM</strong></td>
<td>3</td>
<td>1</td>
<td>L298N (с EN), L293D</td>
<td>2 направления + 1 скорость</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><strong>DIR_DIR</strong></td>
<td>2</td>
<td>0</td>
<td>Реле, простые драйверы</td>
<td>Только вкл/выкл без ШИМ</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table></markdown-accessiblity-table>

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Для режима: DIR_DIR_PWM (3 пина)</span>
<span class="pl-en">AlashMotorControlLite</span>(MODE mode, <span class="pl-c1">uint8_t</span> pin1, <span class="pl-c1">uint8_t</span> pin2, <span class="pl-c1">uint8_t</span> pin_pwm);</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Основные методы</h3><a id="user-content-основные-методы" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Основные методы" href="#основные-методы"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><code>void setSpeed(int16_t speed)</code></h4><a id="user-content-void-setspeedint16_t-speed" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: void setSpeed(int16_t speed)" href="#void-setspeedint16_t-speed"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Установка скорости и направления мотора</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Параметры:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>speed</code> - скорость от <strong>-100 до 100</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>-100</code> до <code>-1</code> = движение назад</li>
<li><code>0</code> = остановка</li>
<li><code>1</code> до <code>100</code> = движение вперед</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Пример:</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++ notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="motor.setSpeed(75);    // Вперед на 75%
motor.setSpeed(-50);   // Назад на 50%
motor.setSpeed(0);     // Остановка"><pre>motor.setSpeed(<span class="pl-c1">75</span>);    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Вперед на 75%</span>
motor.setSpeed(-<span class="pl-c1">50</span>);   <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Назад на 50%</span>
motor.setSpeed(<span class="pl-c1">0</span>);     <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Остановка</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><code>void stop()</code></h4><a id="user-content-void-stop" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: void stop()" href="#void-stop"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Свободная остановка мотора (coast stop)</p>
<p dir="auto">Мотор отключается и останавливается по инерции. Используется для:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Плавной остановки без нагрузки на механику</li>
<li>Экономии энергии</li>
<li>Обычной остановки в конце движения</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Пример:</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++ notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="motor.setSpeed(100);
delay(2000);
motor.stop();  // Плавная остановка"><pre>motor.setSpeed(<span class="pl-c1">100</span>);
<span class="pl-en">delay</span>(<span class="pl-c1">2000</span>);
motor.stop();  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Плавная остановка</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><code>void brake()</code></h4><a id="user-content-void-brake" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: void brake()" href="#void-brake"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Активное торможение мотора</p>
<p dir="auto">Мотор активно тормозит (короткое замыкание обмоток). Используется для:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Быстрой остановки</li>
<li>Удержания позиции под нагрузкой</li>
<li>Точной остановки</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Пример:</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++ notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="motor.setSpeed(100);
delay(2000);
motor.brake();  // Резкое торможение"><pre>motor.setSpeed(<span class="pl-c1">100</span>);
<span class="pl-en">delay</span>(<span class="pl-c1">2000</span>);
motor.brake();  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Резкое торможение</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><code>int16_t getSpeed()</code></h4><a id="user-content-int16_t-getspeed" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: int16_t getSpeed()" href="#int16_t-getspeed"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">💡 Примеры использования</h2><a id="user-content--примеры-использования" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 💡 Примеры использования" href="#-примеры-использования"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Плавный разгон и торможение</h3><a id="user-content-плавный-разгон-и-торможение" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Плавный разгон и торможение" href="#плавный-разгон-и-торможение"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++ notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="#include &quot;AlashMotorControlLite.h&quot;

AlashMotorControlLite motor(DIR_PWM, 4, 3);

void smoothSpeed(int target, int delayMs) {
  int current = motor.getSpeed();
  int step = (target &gt; current) ? 1 : -1;

  for (int speed = current; speed != target; speed += step) {
    motor.setSpeed(speed);
    delay(delayMs);
  }
}

void setup() {}

void loop() {
  smoothSpeed(100, 20);   // Плавный разгон за 2 секунды
  delay(2000);
  smoothSpeed(0, 20);     // Плавное торможение
  delay(1000);
}"><pre>#<span class="pl-k">include</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>AlashMotorControlLite.h<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>

AlashMotorControlLite <span class="pl-en">motor</span>(DIR_PWM, <span class="pl-c1">4</span>, <span class="pl-c1">3</span>);

<span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">smoothSpeed</span>(<span class="pl-k">int</span> target, <span class="pl-k">int</span> delayMs) {
  <span class="pl-k">int</span> current = motor.<span class="pl-c1">getSpeed</span>();
  <span class="pl-k">int</span> step = (target &gt; current) ? <span class="pl-c1">1</span> : -<span class="pl-c1">1</span>;

  <span class="pl-k">for</span> (<span class="pl-k">int</span> speed = current; speed != target; speed += step) {
    motor.<span class="pl-c1">setSpeed</span>(speed);
    <span class="pl-c1">delay</span>(delayMs);
  }
}

<span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">setup</span>() {}

<span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">loop</span>() {
  <span class="pl-c1">smoothSpeed</span>(<span class="pl-c1">100</span>, <span class="pl-c1">20</span>);   <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Плавный разгон за 2 секунды</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">delay</span>(<span class="pl-c1">2000</span>);
  <span class="pl-c1">smoothSpeed</span>(<span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-c1">20</span>);     <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Плавное торможение</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">delay</span>(<span class="pl-c1">1000</span>);
}</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Управление двумя моторами (робот)</h3><a id="user-content-управление-двумя-моторами-робот" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Управление двумя моторами (робот)" href="#управление-двумя-моторами-робот"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++ notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="#include &quot;AlashMotorControlLite.h&quot;

AlashMotorControlLite motorLeft(PWM_PWM, 32, 33);
AlashMotorControlLite motorRight(PWM_PWM, 25, 26);

void moveForward(int speed) {
  motorLeft.setSpeed(speed);
  motorRight.setSpeed(speed);
}

void turnRight(int speed) {
  motorLeft.setSpeed(speed);
  motorRight.setSpeed(-speed);
}

void stopAll() {
  motorLeft.stop();
  motorRight.stop();
}

void setup() {}

void loop() {
  moveForward(70);    // Вперед
  delay(2000);

  turnRight(50);      // Поворот направо
  delay(1000);

  stopAll();          // Остановка
  delay(1000);
}"><pre>#<span class="pl-k">include</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>AlashMotorControlLite.h<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>

AlashMotorControlLite <span class="pl-en">motorLeft</span>(PWM_PWM, <span class="pl-c1">32</span>, <span class="pl-c1">33</span>);
AlashMotorControlLite <span class="pl-en">motorRight</span>(PWM_PWM, <span class="pl-c1">25</span>, <span class="pl-c1">26</span>);

<span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">moveForward</span>(<span class="pl-k">int</span> speed) {
  motorLeft.<span class="pl-c1">setSpeed</span>(speed);
  motorRight.<span class="pl-c1">setSpeed</span>(speed);
}

<span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">turnRight</span>(<span class="pl-k">int</span> speed) {
  motorLeft.<span class="pl-c1">setSpeed</span>(speed);
  motorRight.<span class="pl-c1">setSpeed</span>(-speed);
}

<span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">stopAll</span>() {
  motorLeft.<span class="pl-c1">stop</span>();
  motorRight.<span class="pl-c1">stop</span>();
}

<span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">setup</span>() {}

<span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">loop</span>() {
  <span class="pl-c1">moveForward</span>(<span class="pl-c1">70</span>);    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Вперед</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">delay</span>(<span class="pl-c1">2000</span>);

  <span class="pl-c1">turnRight</span>(<span class="pl-c1">50</span>);      <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Поворот направо</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">delay</span>(<span class="pl-c1">1000</span>);

  <span class="pl-c1">stopAll</span>();          <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Остановка</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">delay</span>(<span class="pl-c1">1000</span>);
}</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Меканум колеса (4WD)</h3><a id="user-content-меканум-колеса-4wd" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Меканум колеса (4WD)" href="#меканум-колеса-4wd"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++ notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="#include &quot;AlashMotorControlLite.h&quot;

AlashMotorControlLite motorFL(PWM_PWM, 32, 33);  // Front Left
AlashMotorControlLite motorFR(PWM_PWM, 25, 26);  // Front Right
AlashMotorControlLite motorRL(PWM_PWM, 19, 18);  // Rear Left
AlashMotorControlLite motorRR(PWM_PWM, 17, 16);  // Rear Right

void mecanumDrive(int vx, int vy, int rotation) {
  int speedFL = vx + vy + rotation;
  int speedFR = vx - vy - rotation;
  int speedRL = vx - vy + rotation;
  int speedRR = vx + vy - rotation;

  motorFL.setSpeed(constrain(speedFL, -100, 100));
  motorFR.setSpeed(constrain(speedFR, -100, 100));
  motorRL.setSpeed(constrain(speedRL, -100, 100));
  motorRR.setSpeed(constrain(speedRR, -100, 100));
}

void setup() {}

void loop() {
  mecanumDrive(50, 0, 0);     // Вперед
  delay(2000);

  mecanumDrive(0, 50, 0);     // Страфинг влево
  delay(2000);

  mecanumDrive(0, 0, 30);     // Поворот на месте
  delay(2000);
}"><pre>#<span class="pl-k">include</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>AlashMotorControlLite.h<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>

AlashMotorControlLite <span class="pl-en">motorFL</span>(PWM_PWM, <span class="pl-c1">32</span>, <span class="pl-c1">33</span>);  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Front Left</span>
AlashMotorControlLite <span class="pl-en">motorFR</span>(PWM_PWM, <span class="pl-c1">25</span>, <span class="pl-c1">26</span>);  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Front Right</span>
AlashMotorControlLite <span class="pl-en">motorRL</span>(PWM_PWM, <span class="pl-c1">19</span>, <span class="pl-c1">18</span>);  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Rear Left</span>
AlashMotorControlLite <span class="pl-en">motorRR</span>(PWM_PWM, <span class="pl-c1">17</span>, <span class="pl-c1">16</span>);  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Rear Right</span>

<span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">mecanumDrive</span>(<span class="pl-k">int</span> vx, <span class="pl-k">int</span> vy, <span class="pl-k">int</span> rotation) {
  <span class="pl-k">int</span> speedFL = vx + vy + rotation;
  <span class="pl-k">int</span> speedFR = vx - vy - rotation;
  <span class="pl-k">int</span> speedRL = vx - vy + rotation;
  <span class="pl-k">int</span> speedRR = vx + vy - rotation;

  motorFL.<span class="pl-c1">setSpeed</span>(<span class="pl-c1">constrain</span>(speedFL, -<span class="pl-c1">100</span>, <span class="pl-c1">100</span>));
  motorFR.<span class="pl-c1">setSpeed</span>(<span class="pl-c1">constrain</span>(speedFR, -<span class="pl-c1">100</span>, <span class="pl-c1">100</span>));
  motorRL.<span class="pl-c1">setSpeed</span>(<span class="pl-c1">constrain</span>(speedRL, -<span class="pl-c1">100</span>, <span class="pl-c1">100</span>));
  motorRR.<span class="pl-c1">setSpeed</span>(<span class="pl-c1">constrain</span>(speedRR, -<span class="pl-c1">100</span>, <span class="pl-c1">100</span>));
}

<span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">setup</span>() {}

<span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">loop</span>() {
  <span class="pl-c1">mecanumDrive</span>(<span class="pl-c1">50</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>);     <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Вперед</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">delay</span>(<span class="pl-c1">2000</span>);

  <span class="pl-c1">mecanumDrive</span>(<span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-c1">50</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>);     <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Страфинг влево</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">delay</span>(<span class="pl-c1">2000</span>);

  <span class="pl-c1">mecanumDrive</span>(<span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-c1">30</span>);     <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Поворот на месте</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">delay</span>(<span class="pl-c1">2000</span>);
}</pre></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">❓ FAQ (Часто задаваемые вопросы)</h2><a id="user-content--faq-часто-задаваемые-вопросы" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: ❓ FAQ (Часто задаваемые вопросы)" href="#-faq-часто-задаваемые-вопросы"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Какой режим выбрать для моего драйвера?</h3><a id="user-content-какой-режим-выбрать-для-моего-драйвера" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Какой режим выбрать для моего драйвера?" href="#какой-режим-выбрать-для-моего-драйвера"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>L298N</strong> → <code>DIR_DIR_PWM</code> (если используете EN пин) или <code>PWM_PWM</code></li>
<li><strong>TB6612FNG</strong> → <code>DIR_PWM</code></li>
<li><strong>ZK-5AD</strong> → <code>PWM_PWM</code></li>
<li><strong>DRV8833</strong> → <code>DIR_PWM</code></li>
<li><strong>BTS7960</strong> → <code>PWM_PWM</code></li>
<li><strong>Реле</strong> → <code>DIR_DIR</code></li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Почему мотор не вращается?</h3><a id="user-content-почему-мотор-не-вращается" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Почему мотор не вращается?" href="#почему-мотор-не-вращается"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Проверьте питание драйвера (должно быть достаточным для мотора)</li>
<li>Убедитесь, что выбран правильный MODE</li>
<li>Проверьте подключение пинов</li>
<li>На ESP32: убедитесь, что используете не только INPUT пины</li>
<li>Попробуйте setSpeed(100) для максимальной скорости</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Мотор вращается в неправильную сторону</h3><a id="user-content-мотор-вращается-в-неправильную-сторону" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Мотор вращается в неправильную сторону" href="#мотор-вращается-в-неправильную-сторону"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Поменяйте местами провода мотора (M+ и M-) или поменяйте pin1 и pin2 в конструкторе:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++ notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// Было
AlashMotorControlLite motor(PWM_PWM, 32, 33);

// Стало (инвертировано)
AlashMotorControlLite motor(PWM_PWM, 33, 32);"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Было</span>

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Стало (инвертировано)</span>
AlashMotorControlLite <span class="pl-en">motor</span>(PWM_PWM, <span class="pl-c1">33</span>, <span class="pl-c1">32</span>);</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Как управлять более чем 2 моторами?</h3><a id="user-content-как-управлять-более-чем-2-моторами" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Как управлять более чем 2 моторами?" href="#как-управлять-более-чем-2-моторами"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Создайте несколько объектов:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++ notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="AlashMotorControlLite motor1(PWM_PWM, 32, 33);

<p dir="auto">ESP32 поддерживает до 16 PWM каналов.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">В чем разница между stop() и brake()?</h3><a id="user-content-в-чем-разница-между-stop-и-brake" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: В чем разница между stop() и brake()?" href="#в-чем-разница-между-stop-и-brake"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>stop()</strong> - свободная остановка (выбег по инерции), меньше нагрузка</li>
<li><strong>brake()</strong> - активное торможение (быстрая остановка), больше нагрузка</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">Используйте <code>stop()</code> для обычной остановки, <code>brake()</code> когда нужна быстрая остановка.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Поддерживается ли ESP32-S3 / ESP32-C3?</h3><a id="user-content-поддерживается-ли-esp32-s3--esp32-c3" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Поддерживается ли ESP32-S3 / ESP32-C3?" href="#поддерживается-ли-esp32-s3--esp32-c3"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Да, библиотека работает на всех вариантах ESP32 (ESP32, ESP32-S2, ESP32-S3, ESP32-C3, ESP32-C6).</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Можно ли использовать с Servo библиотекой?</h3><a id="user-content-можно-ли-использовать-с-servo-библиотекой" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Можно ли использовать с Servo библиотекой?" href="#можно-ли-использовать-с-servo-библиотекой"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Да, но на Arduino будьте осторожны с PWM пинами - Servo и ШИМ могут конфликтовать на одних таймерах. На ESP32 проблем нет.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">🔧 Расширенные возможности</h2><a id="user-content--расширенные-возможности" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 🔧 Расширенные возможности" href="#-расширенные-возможности"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Плавный реверс (безопасная смена направления)</h3><a id="user-content-плавный-реверс-безопасная-смена-направления" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Плавный реверс (безопасная смена направления)" href="#плавный-реверс-безопасная-смена-направления"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++ notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="void safeReverse(int newSpeed) {
  // Текущая скорость
  int current = motor.getSpeed();

  // Если разные знаки - нужен реверс
  if ((current &gt; 0 &amp;&amp; newSpeed &lt; 0) || (current &lt; 0 &amp;&amp; newSpeed &gt; 0)) {
    // Плавно до нуля
    while (abs(motor.getSpeed()) &gt; 0) {
      int speed = motor.getSpeed();
      motor.setSpeed(speed &gt; 0 ? speed - 1 : speed + 1);
      delay(10);
    }

    // Активное торможение
    motor.brake();
    delay(300);

    // Пауза
    motor.stop();
    delay(200);
  }

  // Плавно до новой скорости
  while (motor.getSpeed() != newSpeed) {
    int speed = motor.getSpeed();
    int step = (newSpeed &gt; speed) ? 1 : -1;
    motor.setSpeed(speed + step);
    delay(10);
  }
}"><pre><span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">safeReverse</span>(<span class="pl-k">int</span> newSpeed) {
  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Текущая скорость</span>
  <span class="pl-k">int</span> current = motor.<span class="pl-c1">getSpeed</span>();

  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Если разные знаки - нужен реверс</span>
  <span class="pl-k">if</span> ((current &gt; <span class="pl-c1">0</span> &amp;&amp; newSpeed &lt; <span class="pl-c1">0</span>) || (current &lt; <span class="pl-c1">0</span> &amp;&amp; newSpeed &gt; <span class="pl-c1">0</span>)) {
    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Плавно до нуля</span>
    <span class="pl-k">while</span> (<span class="pl-c1">abs</span>(motor.<span class="pl-c1">getSpeed</span>()) &gt; <span class="pl-c1">0</span>) {
      <span class="pl-k">int</span> speed = motor.<span class="pl-c1">getSpeed</span>();
      motor.<span class="pl-c1">setSpeed</span>(speed &gt; <span class="pl-c1">0</span> ? speed - <span class="pl-c1">1</span> : speed + <span class="pl-c1">1</span>);
      <span class="pl-c1">delay</span>(<span class="pl-c1">10</span>);
    }

    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Активное торможение</span>
    motor.<span class="pl-c1">brake</span>();
    <span class="pl-c1">delay</span>(<span class="pl-c1">300</span>);

    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Пауза</span>
    motor.<span class="pl-c1">stop</span>();
    <span class="pl-c1">delay</span>(<span class="pl-c1">200</span>);
  }

  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Плавно до новой скорости</span>
  <span class="pl-k">while</span> (motor.<span class="pl-c1">getSpeed</span>() != newSpeed) {
    <span class="pl-k">int</span> speed = motor.<span class="pl-c1">getSpeed</span>();
    <span class="pl-k">int</span> step = (newSpeed &gt; speed) ? <span class="pl-c1">1</span> : -<span class="pl-c1">1</span>;
    motor.<span class="pl-c1">setSpeed</span>(speed + step);
    <span class="pl-c1">delay</span>(<span class="pl-c1">10</span>);
  }
}</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Автоматическая калибровка (поиск нуля)</h3><a id="user-content-автоматическая-калибровка-поиск-нуля" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Автоматическая калибровка (поиск нуля)" href="#автоматическая-калибровка-поиск-нуля"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++ notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="void findMinSpeed() {
  Serial.println(&quot;Поиск минимальной скорости...&quot;);

  for (int speed = 0; speed &lt;= 100; speed++) {
    motor.setSpeed(speed);
    delay(100);

    // Здесь можно добавить проверку энкодера
    // если мотор начал вращаться - это минимум
    Serial.print(&quot;Тест: &quot;);
    Serial.println(speed);
  }

  motor.stop();

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">🛠️ Совместимость</h2><a id="user-content-️-совместимость" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 🛠️ Совместимость" href="#️-совместимость"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
